Introduction

Base URL: http://localhost

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Authenticating requests

This API is not authenticated.

Endpoints

POST api/demo

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/demo" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/demo"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/demo

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

POST api/agent/trial

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/agent/trial" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"magni\",
    \"username\": \"possimus\",
    \"password\": \"5;-Mnu=orMZ,`1NXW\",
    \"password_confirmation\": \"mayutxynhsyupxtriyrrxuddmyvcfdcjbqgpgsngiumbbrabofhmmpfnnljtjanh\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/agent/trial"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "magni",
    "username": "possimus",
    "password": "5;-Mnu=orMZ,`1NXW",
    "password_confirmation": "mayutxynhsyupxtriyrrxuddmyvcfdcjbqgpgsngiumbbrabofhmmpfnnljtjanh"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Request      

POST api/agent/trial

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

email   string   

Example: magni

username   string   

Example: possimus

password   string  optional  

This field is required when password_confirmation is present. The value and password_confirmation must match. Must be at least 6 characters. Example: 5;-Mnu=orMZ,1NXW`

password_confirmation   string  optional  

Must be at least 6 characters. Example: mayutxynhsyupxtriyrrxuddmyvcfdcjbqgpgsngiumbbrabofhmmpfnnljtjanh

POST api/login

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"username\": \"voluptate\",
    \"password\": \"aut\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "username": "voluptate",
    "password": "aut"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
Received response:
Request failed with error:


Tip: Check that you're properly connected to the network.
If you're a maintainer of ths API, verify that your API is running and you've enabled CORS.
You can check the Dev Tools console for debugging information.

Example: voluptate

Example: aut

}"

    "http://localhost/api/register"
);

    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

    "username": "e8elf",

Request      

POST api/register

Headers

Content-Type      

Example: application/json

Accept      

Example: application/json

Body Parameters

username   string   

Must match the regex /^[A-Za-z0-9]+$/. Example: e8elf

password   string   

Must be at least 6 characters. Example: _Xt-~|Vhnm.uGxi'a

POST api/password/reset

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/password/reset" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"token\": \"voluptatem\",
    \"email\": \"ubrakus@example.org\",
    \"password\": \"~{mRy#+>p[2\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/password/reset"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

    "token": "voluptatem",
    "email": "ubrakus@example.org",
    "password": "~{mRy#+>p[2"
};

    method: "POST",

POST api/shops/create

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost/api/shops/create" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"vuxttpb\",
    \"country\": \"assumenda\",
    \"os\": \"delectus\",
    \"device\": \"nobis\",
    \"access\": \"quam\"
}"

    "http://localhost/api/shops/create"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

    "name": "vuxttpb",
    "country": "assumenda",
    "os": "delectus",
    "device": "nobis",
    "access": "quam"
};

    method: "POST",

}).then(response => response.json());

curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost/api/player/isonline" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"userid\": \"ut\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost/api/player/isonline"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "userid": "ut"
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
